MSE reduction % = (mean(mse_differences) / MSE_baseline) * 100\\n    \\n    Returns: dict with p_value, ci_95, mse_reduction_pct, mse_differences\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    np.random.seed(random_state)\\n    n = len(y)\\n    \\n    avg_features = ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length']\\n    uniformity_features = ['cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']\\n    combined_features = avg_features + uniformity_features\\n    \\n    mse_differences = []\\n    \\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        # Bootstrap sample\\n        boot_idx = np.random.choice(n, size=n, replace=True)\\n        oob_idx = np.setdiff1d(np.arange(n), boot_idx)\\n        \\n        if len(oob_idx) < 10:  # Need at least 10 OOB samples\\n            continue\\n        \\n        # Scale features per bootstrap sample\\n        scaler_A = StandardScaler()\\n        scaler_B = StandardScaler()\\n        \\n        X_A_boot = scaler_A.fit_transform(X.loc[boot_idx, avg_features])\\n        X_A_oob = scaler_A.transform(X.loc[oob_idx, avg_features])\\n        \\n        X_B_boot = scaler_B.fit_transform(X.loc[boot_idx, combined_features])\\n        X_B_oob = scaler_B.transform(X.loc[oob_idx, combined_features])\\n        \\n        y_boot = y[boot_idx]\\n        y_oob = y[oob_idx]\\n        \\n        # Fit models\\n        model_A = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        model_B = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        \\n        model_A.fit(X_A_boot, y_boot)\\n        model_B.fit(X_B_boot, y_boot)\\n        \\n        # MSE on OOB\\n        mse_A = mean_squared_error(y_oob, model_A.predict(X_A_oob))\\n        mse_B = mean_squared_error(y_oob, model_B.predict(X_B_oob))\\n        \\n        mse_differences.append(mse_A - mse_B)  # Positive = combined model better\\n    \\n    mse_differences = np.array(mse_differences)\\n    \\n    # One-sided p-value (H1: B reduces MSE compared to A)\\n    p_value = np.mean(mse_differences <= 0)\\n    \\n    # Two-sided p-value also reported\\n    p_value_two_sided = 2 * min(p_value, 1 - p_value)\\n    \\n    # 95% CI for MSE difference\\n    ci_lower = np.percentile(mse_differences, 2.5)\\n    ci_upper = np.percentile(mse_differences, 97.5)\\n    \\n    # MSE reduction percentage\\n    mse_baseline = np.mean([mean_squared_error(y, np.full_like(y, np.mean(y)))])\\n    mean_mse_reduction = np.mean(mse_differences)\\n    mse_reduction_pct = (mean_mse_reduction / mse_baseline) * 100\\n    \\n    return {\\n        'p_value_one_sided': p_value,\\n        'p_value_two_sided': p_value_two_sided,\\n        'mse_differences': mse_differences.tolist(),\\n        'ci_95_lower': ci_lower,\\n        'ci_95_upper': ci_upper,\\n        'mean_mse_reduction': mean_mse_reduction,\\n        'mse_reduction_pct': mse_reduction_pct,\\n        'n_valid_bootstrap': len(mse_differences)\\n    }\\n\\n# Run on both datasets\\nresults_weebit = paired_bootstrap_mse_test(X[sources == 'WeeBIT'], y[sources == 'WeeBIT'], 10000)\\nresults_cefr = paired_bootstrap_mse_test(X[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], y[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], 10000)\\n\\nprint(f\\\"WeeBIT: MSE reduction = {results_weebit['mse_reduction_pct']:.2f}%, p = {results_weebit['p_value_one_sided']:.4f}\\\")\\nprint(f\\\"CEFR-SP: MSE reduction = {results_cefr['mse_reduction_pct']:.2f}%, p = {results_cefr['p_value_one_sided']:.4f}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 2: Bootstrap CI for Ridge Regression Coefficients\\n\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coefficient_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000, alpha=0.05, random_state=42):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Bootstrap confidence intervals for model coefficients.\\n    \\n    Approach:\\n    1. For each bootstrap sample, fit Ridge regression\\n    2. Store coefficients\\n    3. Compute percentile CI (default 95%)\\n    4. Check if CI excludes 0 (statistical significance)\\n    \\n    Also computes bootstrap standard error and z-statistic p-value.\\n    \\n    Returns: DataFrame with feature, coef, bootstrap_se, ci_lower, ci_upper, p_value, significant\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    np.random.seed(random_state)\\n    n = len(y)\\n    feature_names = X.columns.tolist()\\n    n_features = len(feature_names)\\n    \\n    coef_matrix = np.zeros((n_bootstrap, n_features))\\n    intercept_vector = np.zeros(n_bootstrap)\\n    \\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        boot_idx = np.random.choice(n, size=n, replace=True)\\n        \\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\\n        X_boot = scaler.fit_transform(X.iloc[boot_idx])\\n        y_boot = y[boot_idx]\\n        \\n        model = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        model.fit(X_boot, y_boot)\\n        \\n        coef_matrix[b, :] = model.coef_\\n        intercept_vector[b] = model.intercept_\\n    \\n    # Compute statistics\\n    results = []\\n    for i, feature in enumerate(feature_names):\\n        coefs = coef_matrix[:, i]\\n        mean_coef = np.mean(coefs)\\n        bootstrap_se = np.std(coefs)\\n        \\n        # Percentile CI\\n        lower = np.percentile(coefs, (alpha/2) * 100)\\n        upper = np.percentile(coefs, (1 - alpha/2) * 100)\\n        \\n        # P-value: proportion of bootstrap samples where coefficient sign differs from mean\\n        if mean_coef >= 0:\\n            p_val = 2 * np.mean(coefs <= 0)\\n        else:\\n            p_val = 2 * np.mean(coefs >= 0)\\n        \\n        # Significance: CI does not include 0\\n        significant = (lower > 0) if mean_coef > 0 else (upper < 0)\\n        \\n        results.append({\\n            'feature': feature,\\n            'mean_coefficient': mean_coef,\\n            'bootstrap_se': bootstrap_se,\\n            'ci_95_lower': lower,\\n            'ci_95_upper': upper,\\n            'p_value': p_val,\\n            'significant': significant\\n        })\\n    \\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n\\n# Run on combined features model\\nX_combined = X[['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length',\\n                'cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']]\\n\\ncoef_ci_weebit = bootstrap_coefficient_ci(X_combined[sources == 'WeeBIT'], y[sources == 'WeeBIT'], 10000)\\ncoef_ci_cefr = bootstrap_coefficient_ci(X_combined[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], y[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], 10000)\\n\\nprint(\\\"WeeBIT coefficient significance:\\\")\\nprint(coef_ci_weebit[coef_ci_weebit['significant']][['feature', 'mean_coefficient', 'ci_95_lower', 'ci_95_upper']])\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 3: Proper Cross-Validation with Train/Test Separation\\n\\n```python\\ndef cross_val_evaluation(X, y, model_type='Ridge', n_splits=5, random_state=42):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Proper cross-validation with clear train/test separation.\\n    **Only test set metrics are reported** (training metrics are NOT reported\\n    to avoid optimistic bias).\\n    \\n    Uses sklearn KFold with shuffle=True.\\n    \\n    Returns: dict with test set metrics (mean, SD, per-fold values)\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    kf = KFold(n_splits=n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=random_state)\\n    \\n    test_mse_folds = []\\n    test_r2_folds = []\\n    test_mae_folds = []\\n    all_predictions = []\\n    all_actuals = []\\n    \\n    for fold, (train_idx, test_idx) in enumerate(kf.split(X)):\\n        X_train, X_test = X.iloc[train_idx], X.iloc[test_idx]\\n        y_train, y_test = y[train_idx], y[test_idx]\\n        \\n        # Scale on training, apply to test\\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\\n        X_train_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)\\n        X_test_scaled = scaler.transform(X_test)\\n        \\n        # Fit on training\\n        if model_type == 'Ridge':\\n            model = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        else:\\n            model = LinearRegression()\\n        \\n        model.fit(X_train_scaled, y_train)\\n        \\n        # Predict test (NO refitting on test!)\\n        y_pred = model.predict(X_test_scaled)\\n        \\n        # Test metrics only\\n        test_mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y_test, y_pred))\\n        test_r2_folds.append(r2_score(y_test, y_pred))\\n        test_mae_folds.append(np.mean(np.abs(y_test - y_pred)))\\n        \\n        all_predictions.extend(y_pred.tolist())\\n        all_actuals.extend(y_test.tolist())\\n    \\n    return {\\n        'test_mse_mean': np.mean(test_mse_folds),\\n        'test_mse_sd': np.std(test_mse_folds),\\n        'test_mse_folds': test_mse_folds,\\n        'test_r2_mean': np.mean(test_r2_folds),\\n        'test_r2_sd': np.std(test_r2_folds),\\n        'test_r2_folds': test_r2_folds,\\n        'test_mae_mean': np.mean(test_mae_folds),\\n        'test_mae_sd': np.std(test_mae_folds),\\n        'test_predictions': all_predictions,\\n        'test_actuals': all_actuals\\n    }\\n\\n# Evaluate three model variants\\nmodels_to_evaluate = {\\n    'average_only': ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length'],\\n    'uniformity_only': ['cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency'],\\n    'combined': ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length',\\n                 'cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']\\n}\\n\\ncv_results = {}\\nfor model_name, features in models_to_evaluate.items():\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\nEvaluating: {model_name}\\\")\\n    cv_results[model_name] = cross_val_evaluation(X[features], y, 'Ridge', 5)\\n    \\n# Print comparison table\\nprint(\\\"\\\\n\\\" + \\\"=\\\"*60)\\nprint(\\\"CROSS-VALIDATED TEST SET PERFORMANCE (mean \u00b1 SD)\\\")\\nprint(\\\"=\\\"*60)\\nfor model_name in ['average_only', 'uniformity_only', 'combined']:\\n    r = cv_results[model_name]\\n    print(f\\\"{model_name:20s}: R\u00b2 = {r['test_r2_mean']:.4f} \u00b1 {r['test_r2_sd']:.4f}, \\\"\\n          f\\\"MSE = {r['test_mse_mean']:.4f} \u00b1 {r['test_mse_sd']:.4f}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 4: Effect Size Analysis\\n\\n```python\\ndef compute_effect_sizes(cv_results, n):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute effect sizes for R\u00b2 improvements.\\n    \\n    Approach 1: R\u00b2 difference as effect size (simple, interpretable)\\n    - Report: mean R\u00b2 difference, 95% bootstrap CI for difference\\n    \\n    Approach 2: Cohen's d for R\u00b2 improvement\\n    - Convert R\u00b2 to correlation: r = sqrt(R\u00b2)\\n    - Compute Cohen's d for the correlation difference\\n    - Interpretation: d = 0.2 (small), 0.5 (medium), 0.8 (large)\\n    \\n    Approach 3: Practical significance via R\u00b2 classification (Cohen, 1988)\\n    - R\u00b2 = 0.01 (small), 0.09 (medium), 0.25 (large)\\n    \\n    Returns: dict with effect size measures\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    r2_avg = np.array(cv_results['average_only']['test_r2_folds'])\\n    r2_combined = np.array(cv_results['combined']['test_r2_folds'])\\n    \\n    # R\u00b2 difference\\n    r2_diff = r2_combined - r2_avg\\n    mean_diff = np.mean(r2_diff)\\n    sd_diff = np.std(r2_diff)\\n    \\n    # Bootstrap CI for R\u00b2 difference\\n    n_folds = len(r2_diff)\\n    r2_diff_boot = []\\n    for b in range(10000):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n_folds, n_folds, replace=True)\\n        r2_diff_boot.append(np.mean(r2_combined[idx] - r2_avg[idx]))\\n    ci_lower = np.percentile(r2_diff_boot, 2.5)\\n    ci_upper = np.percentile(r2_diff_boot, 97.5)\\n    \\n    # Cohen's d for R\u00b2 improvement (using correlation conversion)\\n    # Convert R\u00b2 to correlation, then compute d from correlation\\n    r_avg = np.sqrt(np.maximum(r2_avg, 0))  # Avoid negative R\u00b2\\n    r_combined = np.sqrt(np.maximum(r2_combined, 0))\\n    \\n    # Cohen's d from correlation: d = 2r / sqrt(1 - r^2)\\n    # Compute for each fold, then average\\n    d_values = []\\n    for r_a, r_c in zip(r_avg, r_combined):\\n        if r_a < 1 and r_c < 1:\\n            d_a = 2 * r_a / np.sqrt(1 - r_a**2 + 1e-10)\\n            d_c = 2 * r_c / np.sqrt(1 - r_c**2 + 1e-10)\\n            d_values.append(d_c - d_a)  # Difference in d\\n    \\n    cohens_d = np.mean(d_values) if d_values else 0.0\\n    \\n    # Interpretation\\n    abs_d = abs(cohens_d)\\n    if abs_d < 0.2:\\n        interpretation = 'negligible'\\n    elif abs_d < 0.5:\\n        interpretation = 'small'\\n    elif abs_d < 0.8:\\n        interpretation = 'medium'\\n    else:\\n        interpretation = 'large'\\n    \\n    # Percentage variance explained gained\\n    pct_improvement = (mean_diff / np.mean(r2_avg)) * 100 if np.mean(r2_avg) > 0 else 0\\n    \\n    return {\\n        'r2_difference_mean': mean_diff,\\n        'r2_difference_sd': sd_diff,\\n        'r2_difference_ci_95': (ci_lower, ci_upper),\\n        'cohens_d': cohens_d,\\n        'cohens_d_interpretation': interpretation,\\n        'mse_reduction_pct': (1 - np.mean(r2_combined) / np.mean(r2_avg)) * 100,  # Approximate\\n        'practical_significance': 'large' if mean_diff > 0.05 else ('medium' if mean_diff > 0.02 else 'small')\\n    }\\n\\neffect_sizes_weebit = compute_effect_sizes(\\n    {k: {fold: cv_results[k]['test_r2_folds'][i] for i in range(5)} for k in cv_results},\\n    len(y[sources == 'WeeBIT'])\\n)\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 5: Ablation Study\\n\\n```python\\ndef ablation_study(X, y, n_splits=5):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Ablation study: test each uniformity feature individually.\\n    \\n    Design:\\n    (A) Add-one-in: Start with average features, add one uniformity feature at a time\\n    (B) Remove-one-out: Start with combined features, remove one uniformity feature at a time\\n    \\n    Returns: DataFrame with R\u00b2 for each ablation condition\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    avg_features = ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length']\\n    uniformity_features = ['cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']\\n    \\n    results = []\\n    \\n    # Baseline: average only\\n    baseline = cross_val_evaluation(X[avg_features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n    results.append({\\n        'condition': 'average_only (baseline)',\\n        'features_used': avg_features,\\n        'test_r2_mean': baseline['test_r2_mean'],\\n        'test_r2_sd': baseline['test_r2_sd'],\\n        'r2_above_baseline': 0.0\\n    })\\n    \\n    # Add-one-in ablation\\n    for uf in uniformity_features:\\n        features = avg_features + [uf]\\n        result = cross_val_evaluation(X[features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n        results.append({\\n            'condition': f'average + {uf}',\\n            'features_used': features,\\n            'test_r2_mean': result['test_r2_mean'],\\n            'test_r2_sd': result['test_r2_sd'],\\n            'r2_above_baseline': result['test_r2_mean'] - baseline['test_r2_mean']\\n        })\\n    \\n    # Full combined\\n    combined_features = avg_features + uniformity_features\\n    combined_result = cross_val_evaluation(X[combined_features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n    results.append({\\n        'condition': 'combined (all features)',\\n        'features_used': combined_features,\\n        'test_r2_mean': combined_result['test_r2_mean'],\\n        'test_r2_sd': combined_result['test_r2_sd'],\\n        'r2_above_baseline': combined_result['test_r2_mean'] - baseline['test_r2_mean']\\n    })\\n    \\n    # Remove-one-out ablation\\n    for uf in uniformity_features:\\n        features = [f for f in combined_features if f != uf]\\n        result = cross_val_evaluation(X[features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n        results.append({\\n            'condition': f'combined without {uf}',\\n            'features_used': features,\\n            'test_r2_mean': result['test_r2_mean'],\\n            'test_r2_sd': result['test_r2_sd'],\\n            'r2_drop': combined_result['test_r2_mean'] - result['test_r2_mean']\\n        })\\n    \\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n\\nablation_weebit = ablation_study(X[sources == 'WeeBIT'], y[sources == 'WeeBIT'])\\nablation_cefr = ablation_study(X[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], y[sources == 'CEFR-SP'])\\n\\nprint(\\\"\\\\n\\\" + \\\"=\\\"*60)\\nprint(\\\"ABLATION STUDY RESULTS\\\")\\nprint(\\\"=\\\"*60)\\nprint(ablation_weebit[['condition', 'test_r2_mean', 'r2_above_baseline']].to_string())\\n```\\n\\n## Output Generation: Publication-Ready Tables\\n\\n```python\\ndef generate_method_out(results_dict):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Generate method_out.json with all statistical results.\\n    \\n    Output structure:\\n    {\\n        'experiment_info': {...},\\n        'dataset_summary': {...},\\n        'model_performance': {...},  # Table 1\\n        'bootstrap_mse_test': {...},  # Table 2\\n        'coefficient_ci': {...},  # Table 3\\n        'effect_sizes': {...},  # Table 4\\n        'ablation_results': {...},  # Table 5\\n        'all_results_json_serializable': True\\n    }\\n    \\n    All numpy arrays and DataFrames are converted to lists/dicts for JSON serialization.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    output = {\\n        'experiment_info': {\\n            'description': 'Statistical evaluation of Uniformity Principle for readability',\\n            'n_bootstrap': 10000,\\n            'cv_folds': 5,\\n            'model': 'Ridge (alpha=1.0)',\\n            'random_state': 42\\n        },\\n        'dataset_summary': {\\n            'total_sentences': int(len(y)),\\n            'weebit_sentences': int(np.sum(sources == 'WeeBIT')),\\n            'cefr_sp_sentences': int(np.sum(sources == 'CEFR-SP')),\\n            'score_mean': float(np.mean(y)),\\n            'score_sd': float(np.std(y))\\n        },\\n        'model_performance': {\\n            'weebit': {\\n                'average_only': format_cv_results(cv_results['average_only']),\\n                'uniformity_only': format_cv_results(cv_results['uniformity_only']),\\n                'combined': format_cv_results(cv_results['combined'])\\n            },\\n            'cefr_sp': {\\n                # Same structure\\n            }\\n        },\\n        'bootstrap_mse_test': {\\n            'weebit': results_weebit,\\n            'cefr_sp': results_cefr\\n        },\\n        'coefficient_ci': {\\n            'weebit': coef_ci_weebit.to_dict('records'),\\n            'cefr_sp': coef_ci_cefr.to_dict('records')\\n        },\\n        'effect_sizes': {\\n            'weebit': effect_sizes_weebit,\\n            'cefr_sp': effect_sizes_cefr\\n        },\\n        'ablation_results': {\\n            'weebit': ablation_weebit.to_dict('records'),\\n            'cefr_sp': ablation_cefr.to_dict('records')\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    # Remove non-serializable items (large arrays)\\n    # Keep only summary statistics, not full bootstrap distributions\\n    \\n    with open('method_out.json', 'w') as f:\\n        json.dump(output, f, indent=2, default=str)\\n    \\n    print(\\\"Results saved to method_out.json\\\")\\n\\ndef format_cv_results(cv_dict):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Format CV results for JSON output (exclude predictions).\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    return {\\n        'test_r2_mean': float(cv_dict['test_r2_mean']),\\n        'test_r2_sd': float(cv_dict['test_r2_sd']),\\n        'test_r2_folds': [float(x) for x in cv_dict['test_r2_folds']],\\n        'test_mse_mean': float(cv_dict['test_mse_mean']),\\n        'test_mse_sd': float(cv_dict['test_mse_sd']),\\n        'test_mse_folds': [float(x) for x in cv_dict['test_mse_folds']],\\n        'test_mae_mean': float(cv_dict['test_mae_mean']),\\n        'test_mae_sd': float(cv_dict['test_mae_sd'])\\n    }\\n\\n# Generate output\\ngenerate_method_out(all_results)\\n```\\n\\n## Execution Timeline (6 hours budget)\\n\\n```\\nHour 0-1: Setup and feature computation\\n- Load full_data_out.json from dependency artifact\\n- Install required packages (pronouncing, cmudict, etc.)\\n- Implement syllable counting with CMUdict\\n- Implement word frequency lookup (SUBTLEX-US or fallback)\\n- Compute features for all 13,129 sentences\\n- Save computed features to features.pkl (avoid recomputation)\\n\\nHour 1-2: Experiment 1 (Bootstrap MSE test)\\n- Implement paired_bootstrap_mse_test function\\n- Run 10,000 bootstrap samples for WeeBIT (3,125 sentences)\\n- Run 10,000 bootstrap samples for CEFR-SP (10,004 sentences)\\n- Compute p-values and confidence intervals\\n\\nHour 2-3: Experiment 2 (Coefficient CI)\\n- Implement bootstrap_coefficient_ci function\\n- Run 10,000 bootstrap samples for both datasets\\n- Identify significant uniformity features\\n\\nHour 3-4: Experiment 3 (Cross-validation)\\n- Implement proper CV with train/test separation\\n- Evaluate all 3 model variants (average, uniformity, combined)\\n- Verify test R\u00b2 matches expected values (~0.226 WeeBIT, ~0.similar for CEFR)\\n\\nHour 4-5: Experiments 4-5 (Effect size + Ablation)\\n- Compute effect sizes (R\u00b2 difference, Cohen's d)\\n- Run ablation studies p-values, R\u00b2 improvements, coefficient signs\\n- Write summary report (results_summary.txt)\\n```\"",
  "new_str": "{\n  \"title\": \"Statistical evaluation of uniformity features for readability\",\n  \"summary\": \"Comprehensive statistical evaluation of the Uniformity Principle hypothesis: bootstrap significance tests for MSE reduction, feature coefficient uncertainty quantification, proper train/test reporting, effect size analysis (Cohen's d), and ablation studies to identify which uniformity features contribute uniquely to readability prediction.\",\n  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"cpu_light\",\n  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"EXPERIMENT OVERVIEW\\n\\nThis experiment conducts comprehensive statistical evaluation of the Uniformity Principle hypothesis using WeeBIT (3,125 sentences) and CEFR-SP (10,004 sentences) datasets.\\n\\nFive experiments:\\n1. Paired Bootstrap Test: Test MSE reduction (17.8% WeeBIT, 8.9% CEFR-SP) with 10,000 bootstrap samples\\n2. Coefficient CI: Bootstrap 95% confidence intervals for Ridge regression coefficients\\n3. Proper CV: 5-fold cross-validation with train/test separation (report test metrics only)\\n4. Effect Size: R\u00b2 improvement with 95% CI, Cohen's d for practical significance\\n5. Ablation: Add-one-in and remove-one-out uniformity feature analysis\\n\\n\\nSTEP 1: DATA LOADING AND FEATURE COMPUTATION\\n\\n```python\\nimport json, numpy as np, pandas as pd\\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import KFold\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error, r2_score\\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\\nimport pronouncing  # CMUdict for syllable counting\\n\\n# Load datasets from dependency artifact\\ndef load_datasets():\\n    with open('full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    sentences, scores, sources = [], [], []\\n    for dataset in data['datasets']:\\n        for ex in dataset['examples']:\\n            sentences.append(ex['input'])\\n            scores.append(float(ex['output']))\\n            sources.append(dataset['dataset'])\\n    return sentences, np.array(scores), np.array(sources)\\n\\nsentences, y, sources = ['avg_word_length','avg_syllables','avg_frequency','sentence_length']\\n    unif_feats = ['cv_word_length','cv_syllables','cv_frequency']\\n    combined = avg_feats + unif_feats\\n    mse_diffs = []\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n, n, replace=True)\\n        oob = np.setdiff1d(np.arange(n), idx)\\n        if len(oob) < 10: continue\\n        sa =   mB = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(sb.transform(X.loc[idx,combined]), y[idx])\\n        mse_A = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mA.predict(sa.transform(X.loc[oob,avg_feats])))\\n        mse_B =   'mse_reduction_pct': (np.mean(mse_diffs)/np.mean((y-np.mean(y))**2))*100\\n    }\\n```\\n\\nSTEP 3: BOOTSTRAP COEFFICIENT CI\\n\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coef_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n StandardScaler()\\n        Xs = scaler.fit_transform(X.iloc[idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(Xs, y[idx])\\n        coefs[b] = model.coef_\\n    results = []\\n    for i, f in enumerate(X.columns):\\n        c = coefs[:,i]\\n        results.append({'feature': f, 'mean_coef': np.mean(c),\\n            'ci_95': (np.percentile(c,2.5), np.percentile(c,97.5)),\\n            'significant': (np.percentile(c,2.5)>0) if np.mean(c)>0 else (np.percentile(c,97.5)<0)})\\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n```\\n\\nSTEP 4: CROSS-VALIDATION (TRAIN/TEST SEPARATION)\\n\\n```python\\ndef cv_evaluate(X, y, n_splits=5):\\n    kf = KFold(n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\\n    r2_folds, mse_folds = [], []\\n    for train_idx, test_idx in {'test_r2_mean': np.mean(r2_folds), 'test_r2_sd': np.std(r2_folds),\\n            'test_mse_mean': np.mean(mse_folds), 'test_mse_sd': np.std(mse_folds)}\\n```\\n\\nSTEP 5: ABLATION cv_evaluate(X[avg], y)\\n\\n# Add-one-in: average + one uniformity feature\\nfor uf in unif:\\n    r = cv_evaluate(X[avg+[uf]], y)\\n    print(f'Average + {uf}: R\u00b2 = {r[\\\"test_r2_mean\\\"]:.4f} (+{r[\\\"test_r2_mean\\\"]-r_avg[\\\"test_r2_mean\\\"]:.4f})')\\n\\n# Full combined\\nr_comb = cv_evaluate(X[avg+unif], y)\\nprint(f'Combined: R\u00b2 = {r_comb[\\\"test_r2_mean\\\"]:.4f} (+{r_comb[\\\"test_r2_mean\\\"]-r_avg[\\\"test_r2_mean\\\"]:.4f})')\\n```\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"FALLBACK STRATEGIES\\n\\n1. The evaluation addresses five key statistical requirements: (1) paired bootstrap test for MSE reduction significance, (2) bootstrap CI for feature coefficients, (3) proper train/test reporting, (4) effect size analysis, and (5) ablation studies.\\n\\n**Key Statistical Approaches**:\\n- Bootstrap hypothesis testing (10,000 samples) for MSE reduction significance\\n- Bootstrap percentile confidence intervals for Ridge regression coefficients\\n- 5-fold cross-validation with proper train/test separation (reporting test metrics only)\\n- Effect size: R\u00b2 improvement with 95% CI, and Cohen's d for practical significance\\n- Ablation: add-one-in and remove-one-out uniformity feature analysis\\n\\n## Data Loading and Feature Computation\\n\\n```python\\nimport json\\nimport numpy as np\\nimport pandas as pd\\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import KFold\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error, r2_score\\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\\nimport scipy.stats as stats\\nimport pronouncing  # For CMUdict syllable counting\\n\\n# Load datasets from dependency artifact\\ndef load_datasets():\\n    with open('full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    \\n    sentences = []\\n    scores = []\\n    sources = []\\n    \\n    for dataset in data['datasets']:\\n        for example in dataset['examples']:\\n            sentences.append(example['input'])\\n            # Heuristic fallback: count vowel groups\\n        vowels = 'aeiouy'\\n        count = 0\\n        prev_was_vowel = False\\n        for char in word:\\n            is_vowel = char in vowels\\n            if is_vowel and not prev_was_vowel:\\n                count += 1\\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\\n        if word.endswith('e'):\\n            count = max(1, count - 1)\\n        return max(1, count)\\n\\ndef get_word_frequency(word):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Get word frequency using SUBTLEX-US norms or NLTK fallback.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    # Implementation: load SUBTLEX-US data from file or use NLTK frequencies\\n    # Return log frequency (higher = more frequent = easier)\\n    pass  # Detailed implementation in executor\\n\\ndef extract_features(sentences):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute both average and uniformity (CV) features for each sentence.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    features_list = []\\n    for sent in sentences:\\n        words = [w for w in sent.split() if w]  # Remove empty strings\\n        if len(words) == 0:\\n            features_list.append({f: 0.0 for f in ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', \\n                                                      'cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency',\\n                                                      'sentence_length']})\\n            continue\\n        \\n        # Word lengths\\n        word_lengths = np.array([len(w) for w in words])\\n        avg_wl = np.mean(word_lengths)\\n        cv_wl = np.std(word_lengths) / (avg_wl + 1e-10)\\n        \\n        # Syllable counts\\n        syll_counts = np.array([syllable_count(w) for w in words])\\n        avg_syll = np.mean(syll_counts)\\n        cv_syll = np.std(syll_counts) / (avg_syll + 1e-10)\\n        \\n        # Word frequencies\\n        freqs = np.array([get_word_frequency(w) for w in words])\\n        avg_freq = np.mean(freqs)\\n        cv_freq = np.std(freqs) / (avg_freq + 1e-10)\\n        \\n        features_list.append({\\n            'avg_word_length': avg_wl,\\n            'avg_syllables': avg_syll,\\n            'avg_frequency': avg_freq,\\n            'cv_word_length': cv_wl,\\n            'cv_syllables': cv_syll,\\n            'cv_frequency': cv_freq,\\n            'sentence_length': len(words)\\n        })\\n    \\n    return pd.DataFrame(features_list)\\n\\nX = extract_features(sentences)\\nprint(f\\\"Features shape: {X.shape}\\\")\\nprint(f\\\"Any NaN? {X.isnull().any().any()}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 1: Paired Bootstrap Test for MSE Reduction Significance\\n\\n```python\\ndef paired_bootstrap_mse_test(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000, random_state=42):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Paired bootstrap test for whether adding uniformity features reduces MSE.\\n    \\n    H0: Adding uniformity features does NOT reduce MSE (MSE_combined >= MSE_average)\\n    H1: Adding uniformity features reduces MSE (MSE_combined < MSE_average)\\n    \\n    Approach (out-of-bag bootstrap):\\n    1. For each bootstrap iteration b:\\n       - Sample n indices with replacement from [0, n-1]\\n       - Fit Model A (average features) and Model B (combined) on bootstrap sample\\n       - Predict on out-of-bag (OOB) samples\\n       - Compute MSE_A and MSE_B on OOB\\n       - Record: mse_diff = MSE_A - MSE_B (positive = B better)\\n    \\n    2. One-sided p-value = proportion of bootstrap samples where mse_diff <= 0\\n       (i.e., proportion where B is NOT better)\\n    \\n    3. 95% CI for MSE difference = [2.5 percentile, 97.5 percentile] of mse_differences\\n    \\n    4. MSE reduction % = (mean(mse_differences) / MSE_baseline) * 100\\n    \\n    Returns: dict with p_value, ci_95, mse_reduction_pct, mse_differences\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    np.random.seed(random_state)\\n    n = len(y)\\n    \\n    avg_features = ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length']\\n    uniformity_features = ['cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']\\n    combined_features = avg_features + uniformity_features\\n    \\n    mse_differences = []\\n    \\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        # Bootstrap sample\\n        boot_idx = np.random.choice(n, size=n, replace=True)\\n        oob_idx = np.setdiff1d(np.arange(n), boot_idx)\\n        \\n        if len(oob_idx) < 10:  # Need at least 10 OOB samples\\n            continue\\n        \\n        # Scale features per bootstrap sample\\n        scaler_A = StandardScaler()\\n        scaler_B = StandardScaler()\\n        \\n        X_A_boot = scaler_A.fit_transform(X.loc[boot_idx, avg_features])\\n        X_A_oob = scaler_A.transform(X.loc[oob_idx, avg_features])\\n        \\n        X_B_boot = scaler_B.fit_transform(X.loc[boot_idx, combined_features])\\n        X_B_oob = scaler_B.transform(X.loc[oob_idx, combined_features])\\n        \\n        y_boot = y[boot_idx]\\n        y_oob = y[oob_idx]\\n        \\n        # Fit models\\n        model_A = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        model_B = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        \\n        model_A.fit(X_A_boot, y_boot)\\n        model_B.fit(X_B_boot, y_boot)\\n        \\n        # MSE on OOB\\n        mse_A = mean_squared_error(y_oob, model_A.predict(X_A_oob))\\n        mse_B = mean_squared_error(y_oob, model_B.predict(X_B_oob))\\n        \\n        mse_differences.append(mse_A - mse_B)  # Positive = combined model better\\n    \\n    mse_differences = np.array(mse_differences)\\n    \\n    # One-sided p-value (H1: B reduces MSE compared to A)\\n    p_value = np.mean(mse_differences <= 0)\\n    \\n    # Two-sided p-value also reported\\n    p_value_two_sided = 2 * min(p_value, 1 - p_value)\\n    \\n    # 95% CI for MSE difference\\n    ci_lower = np.percentile(mse_differences, 2.5)\\n    ci_upper = np.percentile(mse_differences, 97.5)\\n    \\n    # MSE reduction percentage\\n    mse_baseline = np.mean([mean_squared_error(y, np.full_like(y, np.mean(y)))])\\n    mean_mse_reduction = np.mean(mse_differences)\\n    mse_reduction_pct = (mean_mse_reduction / mse_baseline) * 100\\n    \\n    return {\\n        'p_value_one_sided': p_value,\\n        'p_value_two_sided': p_value_two_sided,\\n        'mse_differences': mse_differences.tolist(),\\n        'ci_95_lower': ci_lower,\\n        'ci_95_upper': ci_upper,\\n        'mean_mse_reduction': mean_mse_reduction,\\n        'mse_reduction_pct': mse_reduction_pct,\\n        'n_valid_bootstrap': len(mse_differences)\\n    }\\n\\n# Run on both datasets\\nresults_weebit = paired_bootstrap_mse_test(X[sources == 'WeeBIT'], y[sources == 'WeeBIT'], 10000)\\nresults_cefr = paired_bootstrap_mse_test(X[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], y[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], 10000)\\n\\nprint(f\\\"WeeBIT: MSE reduction = {results_weebit['mse_reduction_pct']:.2f}%, p = {results_weebit['p_value_one_sided']:.4f}\\\")\\nprint(f\\\"CEFR-SP: MSE reduction = {results_cefr['mse_reduction_pct']:.2f}%, p = {results_cefr['p_value_one_sided']:.4f}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 2: Bootstrap CI for Ridge Regression Coefficients\\n\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coefficient_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000, alpha=0.05, random_state=42):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Bootstrap confidence intervals for model coefficients.\\n    \\n    Approach:\\n    1. For each bootstrap sample, fit Ridge regression\\n    2. Store coefficients\\n    3. Compute percentile CI (default 95%)\\n    4. Check if CI excludes 0 (statistical significance)\\n    \\n    Also computes bootstrap standard error and z-statistic p-value.\\n    \\n    Returns: DataFrame with feature, coef, bootstrap_se, ci_lower, ci_upper, p_value, significant\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    np.random.seed(random_state)\\n    n = len(y)\\n    feature_names = X.columns.tolist()\\n    n_features = len(feature_names)\\n    \\n    coef_matrix = np.zeros((n_bootstrap, n_features))\\n    intercept_vector = np.zeros(n_bootstrap)\\n    \\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        boot_idx = np.random.choice(n, size=n, replace=True)\\n        \\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\\n        X_boot = scaler.fit_transform(X.iloc[boot_idx])\\n        y_boot = y[boot_idx]\\n        \\n        model = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        model.fit(X_boot, y_boot)\\n        \\n        coef_matrix[b, :] = model.coef_\\n        intercept_vector[b] = model.intercept_\\n    \\n    # Compute statistics\\n    results = []\\n    for i, feature in enumerate(feature_names):\\n        coefs = coef_matrix[:, i]\\n        mean_coef = np.mean(coefs)\\n        bootstrap_se = np.std(coefs)\\n        \\n        # Percentile CI\\n        lower = np.percentile(coefs, (alpha/2) * 100)\\n        upper = np.percentile(coefs, (1 - alpha/2) * 100)\\n        \\n        # P-value: proportion of bootstrap samples where coefficient sign differs from mean\\n        if mean_coef >= 0:\\n            p_val = 2 * np.mean(coefs <= 0)\\n        else:\\n            p_val = 2 * np.mean(coefs >= 0)\\n        \\n        # Significance: CI does not include 0\\n        significant = (lower > 0) if mean_coef > 0 else (upper < 0)\\n        \\n        results.append({\\n            'feature': feature,\\n            'mean_coefficient': mean_coef,\\n            'bootstrap_se': bootstrap_se,\\n            'ci_95_lower': lower,\\n            'ci_95_upper': upper,\\n            'p_value': p_val,\\n            'significant': significant\\n        })\\n    \\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n\\n# Run on combined features model\\nX_combined = X[['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length',\\n                'cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']]\\n\\ncoef_ci_weebit = bootstrap_coefficient_ci(X_combined[sources == 'WeeBIT'], y[sources == 'WeeBIT'], 10000)\\ncoef_ci_cefr = bootstrap_coefficient_ci(X_combined[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], y[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], 10000)\\n\\nprint(\\\"WeeBIT coefficient significance:\\\")\\nprint(coef_ci_weebit[coef_ci_weebit['significant']][['feature', 'mean_coefficient', 'ci_95_lower', 'ci_95_upper']])\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 3: Proper Cross-Validation with Train/Test Separation\\n\\n```python\\ndef cross_val_evaluation(X, y, model_type='Ridge', n_splits=5, random_state=42):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Proper cross-validation with clear train/test separation.\\n    **Only test set metrics are reported** (training metrics are NOT reported\\n    to avoid optimistic bias).\\n    \\n    Uses sklearn KFold with shuffle=True.\\n    \\n    Returns: dict with test set metrics (mean, SD, per-fold values)\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    kf = KFold(n_splits=n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=random_state)\\n    \\n    test_mse_folds = []\\n    test_r2_folds = []\\n    test_mae_folds = []\\n    all_predictions = []\\n    all_actuals = []\\n    \\n    for fold, (train_idx, test_idx) in enumerate(kf.split(X)):\\n        X_train, X_test = X.iloc[train_idx], X.iloc[test_idx]\\n        y_train, y_test = y[train_idx], y[test_idx]\\n        \\n        # Scale on training, apply to test\\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\\n        X_train_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)\\n        X_test_scaled = scaler.transform(X_test)\\n        \\n        # Fit on training\\n        if model_type == 'Ridge':\\n            model = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)\\n        else:\\n            model = LinearRegression()\\n        \\n        model.fit(X_train_scaled, y_train)\\n        \\n        # Predict test (NO refitting on test!)\\n        y_pred = model.predict(X_test_scaled)\\n        \\n        # Test metrics only\\n        test_mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y_test, y_pred))\\n        test_r2_folds.append(r2_score(y_test, y_pred))\\n        test_mae_folds.append(np.mean(np.abs(y_test - y_pred)))\\n        \\n        all_predictions.extend(y_pred.tolist())\\n        all_actuals.extend(y_test.tolist())\\n    \\n    return {\\n        'test_mse_mean': np.mean(test_mse_folds),\\n        'test_mse_sd': np.std(test_mse_folds),\\n        'test_mse_folds': test_mse_folds,\\n        'test_r2_mean': np.mean(test_r2_folds),\\n        'test_r2_sd': np.std(test_r2_folds),\\n        'test_r2_folds': test_r2_folds,\\n        'test_mae_mean': np.mean(test_mae_folds),\\n        'test_mae_sd': np.std(test_mae_folds),\\n        'test_predictions': all_predictions,\\n        'test_actuals': all_actuals\\n    }\\n\\n# Evaluate three model variants\\nmodels_to_evaluate = {\\n    'average_only': ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length'],\\n    'uniformity_only': ['cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency'],\\n    'combined': ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length',\\n                 'cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']\\n}\\n\\ncv_results = {}\\nfor model_name, features in models_to_evaluate.items():\\n    print(f\\\"\\\\nEvaluating: {model_name}\\\")\\n    cv_results[model_name] = cross_val_evaluation(X[features], y, 'Ridge', 5)\\n    \\n# Print comparison table\\nprint(\\\"\\\\n\\\" + \\\"=\\\"*60)\\nprint(\\\"CROSS-VALIDATED TEST SET PERFORMANCE (mean \u00b1 SD)\\\")\\nprint(\\\"=\\\"*60)\\nfor model_name in ['average_only', 'uniformity_only', 'combined']:\\n    r = cv_results[model_name]\\n    print(f\\\"{model_name:20s}: R\u00b2 = {r['test_r2_mean']:.4f} \u00b1 {r['test_r2_sd']:.4f}, \\\"\\n          f\\\"MSE = {r['test_mse_mean']:.4f} \u00b1 {r['test_mse_sd']:.4f}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 4: Effect Size Analysis\\n\\n```python\\ndef compute_effect_sizes(cv_results, n):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Compute effect sizes for R\u00b2 improvements.\\n    \\n    Approach 1: R\u00b2 difference as effect size (simple, interpretable)\\n    - Report: mean R\u00b2 difference, 95% bootstrap CI for difference\\n    \\n    Approach 2: Cohen's d for R\u00b2 improvement\\n    - Convert R\u00b2 to correlation: r = sqrt(R\u00b2)\\n    - Compute Cohen's d for the correlation difference\\n    - Interpretation: d = 0.2 (small), 0.5 (medium), 0.8 (large)\\n    \\n    Approach 3: Practical significance via R\u00b2 classification (Cohen, 1988)\\n    - R\u00b2 = 0.01 (small), 0.09 (medium), 0.25 (large)\\n    \\n    Returns: dict with effect size measures\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    r2_avg = np.array(cv_results['average_only']['test_r2_folds'])\\n    r2_combined = np.array(cv_results['combined']['test_r2_folds'])\\n    \\n    # R\u00b2 difference\\n    r2_diff = r2_combined - r2_avg\\n    mean_diff = np.mean(r2_diff)\\n    sd_diff = np.std(r2_diff)\\n    \\n    # Bootstrap CI for R\u00b2 difference\\n    n_folds = len(r2_diff)\\n    r2_diff_boot = []\\n    for b in range(10000):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n_folds, n_folds, replace=True)\\n        r2_diff_boot.append(np.mean(r2_combined[idx] - r2_avg[idx]))\\n    ci_lower = np.percentile(r2_diff_boot, 2.5)\\n    ci_upper = np.percentile(r2_diff_boot, 97.5)\\n    \\n    # Cohen's d for R\u00b2 improvement (using correlation conversion)\\n    # Convert R\u00b2 to correlation, then compute d from correlation\\n    r_avg = np.sqrt(np.maximum(r2_avg, 0))  # Avoid negative R\u00b2\\n    r_combined = np.sqrt(np.maximum(r2_combined, 0))\\n    \\n    # Cohen's d from correlation: d = 2r / sqrt(1 - r^2)\\n    # Compute for each fold, then average\\n    d_values = []\\n    for r_a, r_c in zip(r_avg, r_combined):\\n        if r_a < 1 and r_c < 1:\\n            d_a = 2 * r_a / np.sqrt(1 - r_a**2 + 1e-10)\\n            d_c = 2 * r_c / np.sqrt(1 - r_c**2 + 1e-10)\\n            d_values.append(d_c - d_a)  # Difference in d\\n    \\n    cohens_d = np.mean(d_values) if d_values else 0.0\\n    \\n    # Interpretation\\n    abs_d = abs(cohens_d)\\n    if abs_d < 0.2:\\n        interpretation = 'negligible'\\n    elif abs_d < 0.5:\\n        interpretation = 'small'\\n    elif abs_d < 0.8:\\n        interpretation = 'medium'\\n    else:\\n        interpretation = 'large'\\n    \\n    # Percentage variance explained gained\\n    pct_improvement = (mean_diff / np.mean(r2_avg)) * 100 if np.mean(r2_avg) > 0 else 0\\n    \\n    return {\\n        'r2_difference_mean': mean_diff,\\n        'r2_difference_sd': sd_diff,\\n        'r2_difference_ci_95': (ci_lower, ci_upper),\\n        'cohens_d': cohens_d,\\n        'cohens_d_interpretation': interpretation,\\n        'mse_reduction_pct': (1 - np.mean(r2_combined) / np.mean(r2_avg)) * 100,  # Approximate\\n        'practical_significance': 'large' if mean_diff > 0.05 else ('medium' if mean_diff > 0.02 else 'small')\\n    }\\n\\neffect_sizes_weebit = compute_effect_sizes(\\n    {k: {fold: cv_results[k]['test_r2_folds'][i] for i in range(5)} for k in cv_results},\\n    len(y[sources == 'WeeBIT'])\\n)\\n```\\n\\n## Experiment 5: Ablation Study\\n\\n```python\\ndef ablation_study(X, y, n_splits=5):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Ablation study: test each uniformity feature individually.\\n    \\n    Design:\\n    (A) Add-one-in: Start with average features, add one uniformity feature at a time\\n    (B) Remove-one-out: Start with combined features, remove one uniformity feature at a time\\n    \\n    Returns: DataFrame with R\u00b2 for each ablation condition\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    avg_features = ['avg_word_length', 'avg_syllables', 'avg_frequency', 'sentence_length']\\n    uniformity_features = ['cv_word_length', 'cv_syllables', 'cv_frequency']\\n    \\n    results = []\\n    \\n    # Baseline: average only\\n    baseline = cross_val_evaluation(X[avg_features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n    results.append({\\n        'condition': 'average_only (baseline)',\\n        'features_used': avg_features,\\n        'test_r2_mean': baseline['test_r2_mean'],\\n        'test_r2_sd': baseline['test_r2_sd'],\\n        'r2_above_baseline': 0.0\\n    })\\n    \\n    # Add-one-in ablation\\n    for uf in uniformity_features:\\n        features = avg_features + [uf]\\n        result = cross_val_evaluation(X[features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n        results.append({\\n            'condition': f'average + {uf}',\\n            'features_used': features,\\n            'test_r2_mean': result['test_r2_mean'],\\n            'test_r2_sd': result['test_r2_sd'],\\n            'r2_above_baseline': result['test_r2_mean'] - baseline['test_r2_mean']\\n        })\\n    \\n    # Full combined\\n    combined_features = avg_features + uniformity_features\\n    combined_result = cross_val_evaluation(X[combined_features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n    results.append({\\n        'condition': 'combined (all features)',\\n        'features_used': combined_features,\\n        'test_r2_mean': combined_result['test_r2_mean'],\\n        'test_r2_sd': combined_result['test_r2_sd'],\\n        'r2_above_baseline': combined_result['test_r2_mean'] - baseline['test_r2_mean']\\n    })\\n    \\n    # Remove-one-out ablation\\n    for uf in uniformity_features:\\n        features = [f for f in combined_features if f != uf]\\n        result = cross_val_evaluation(X[features], y, 'Ridge', n_splits)\\n        results.append({\\n            'condition': f'combined without {uf}',\\n            'features_used': features,\\n            'test_r2_mean': result['test_r2_mean'],\\n            'test_r2_sd': result['test_r2_sd'],\\n            'r2_drop': combined_result['test_r2_mean'] - result['test_r2_mean']\\n        })\\n    \\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n\\nablation_weebit = ablation_study(X[sources == 'WeeBIT'], y[sources == 'WeeBIT'])\\nablation_cefr = ablation_study(X[sources == 'CEFR-SP'], y[sources == 'CEFR-SP'])\\n\\nprint(\\\"\\\\n\\\" + \\\"=\\\"*60)\\nprint(\\\"ABLATION STUDY RESULTS\\\")\\nprint(\\\"=\\\"*60)\\nprint(ablation_weebit[['condition', 'test_r2_mean', 'r2_above_baseline']].to_string())\\n```\\n\\n## Output Generation: Publication-Ready Tables\\n\\n```python\\ndef generate_method_out(results_dict):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Generate method_out.json with all statistical results.\\n    \\n    Output structure:\\n    {\\n        'experiment_info': {...},\\n        'dataset_summary': {...},\\n        'model_performance': {...},  # Table 1\\n n = len(y)\\n    avg_feats = ['avg_word_length','avg_syllables','avg_frequency','sentence_length']\\n    unif_feats = ['cv_word_length','cv_syllables','cv_frequency']\\n    combined = avg_feats + unif_feats\\n    mse_diffs = []\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n, n, replace=True)\\n        oob = np.setdiff1d(np.arange(n), idx)\\n        if len(oob) < 10: mA.predict(sa.transform(X.loc[oob,avg_feats])))\\n        mse_B = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mB.predict(sb.transform(X.loc[oob,combined])))\\n        mse_diffs.append(mse_A - mse_B)\\n    mse_diffs = 'mse_reduction_pct': (np.mean(mse_diffs)/np.mean((y-np.mean(y))**2))*100\\n    }\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 2: BOOTSTRAP COEFFICIENT CI\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coef_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n StandardScaler()\\n        Xs = scaler.fit_transform(X.iloc[idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(Xs, y[idx])\\n        coefs[b] = model.coef_\\n    results = []\\n    for i, f in enumerate(X.columns):\\n        c = coefs[:,i]\\n        results.append({'feature': f, 'mean_coef': np.mean(c),\\n            'ci_95': (np.percentile(c,2.5), np.percentile(c,97.5)),\\n            'significant': (np.percentile(c,2.5)>0) if np.mean(c)>0 else (np.percentile(c,97.5)<0)})\\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 3: CROSS-VALIDATION (TRAIN/TEST SEPARATION)\\n```python\\ndef cv_evaluate(X, y, n_splits=5):\\n    kf = KFold(n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\\n    r2_folds, mse_folds = [], []\\n    for train_idx, test_idx in kf.split(X):\\n        scaler = StandardScaler().fit(X.iloc[train_idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(scaler.transform(X.iloc[train_idx]), y[train_idx])\\n        y_pred = model.predict(scaler.transform(X.iloc[test_idx]))\\n        r2_folds.append(r2_score(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n        mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n    return {'test_r2_mean': np.mean(r2_folds), 'test_r2_sd': np.std(r2_folds),\\n            'test_mse_mean': np.mean(mse_folds), 'test_mse_sd': np.std(mse_folds)}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 4: EFFECT SIZE ANALYSIS\\n- Compute R\u00b2 difference (combined - average) with bootstrap 95% CI\\n- Convert R\u00b2 to correlation: r = sqrt(R\u00b2)\\n- Compute Cohen's d: d = 2r / sqrt(1 - r^2)\\n- Interpretation: d=0.2 (small), 0.5 (medium), 0.8 (large)\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 5: ABLATION STUDY\\n- Baseline: average features only\\n- Add-one-in: average + one uniformity feature at a time\\n- Remove-one-out: combined minus one uniformity feature at a time\\n- Report R\u00b2 for each condition\\n\\nOUTPUT: method_out.json with all results in publication-ready format.\",\n    \"fallback_plan\": \"FALLBACK STRATEGIES FOR COMMON ISSUES\\n\\n1.     coefs[b] = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(Xs, y[idx]).coef_\\n    return pd.DataFrame([{'feature': f, 'mean_coef': np.mean(coefs[:,i]), 'ci_95': np.percentile(coefs[:,i], [2.5, 97.5]).tolist(), Cross-Validation\\n```python\\ndef cv_evaluate(X, y):\\n    kf = KFold(5, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\\n    r2_folds, mse_folds = [], []\\n    for train_idx, test_idx in kf.split(X):\\n        scaler = StandardScaler().fit(X.iloc[train_idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(scaler.transform(X.iloc[train_idx]), y[train_idx])\\n        y_pred = model.predict(scaler.transform(X.iloc[test_idx]))\\n        r2_folds.append(r2_score(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n        mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n    return {'test_r2_mean': np.mean(r2_folds), 'test_r2_sd': np.std(r2_folds), 'test_mse_mean': np.mean(mse_folds), 'test_mse_sd': np.std(mse_folds)}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 4-5: Effect sizes and ablation\\n- Compute R\u00b2 difference with bootstrap CI\\n- Cohen's d = 2*r/sqrt(1-r\u00b2) where r=sqrt(R\u00b2)\\n- Ablation: test each uniformity feature individually\\n\\nOUTPUT: method_out.json with all results.\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"FALLBACK STRATEGIES\\n\\n1. SLOW BOOTSTRAP: Reduce to 1,000 bootstrap samples (valid per statistical literature). Or use permutation test (999 permutations) which is faster.\\n\\n2. CMUDICT OOV: Use heuristic syllable counting fallback - count vowel groups (a,e,i,o,u,y) with silent-e adjustment.\\n\\n3. NO SUBTLEX-US: Use NLTK Gutenberg frequencies: from nltk.corpus import gutenberg; freq = Counter(gutenberg.words()); normalize as log(1+count)/total.\\n\\n4. MULTICOLLINEARITY: Check VIF; if VIF>10 remove correlated features. Or use Lasso for feature selection.\\n\\n5. WIDE CI: Use BCa bootstrap via scipy.stats.bootstrap(method='BCa').\\n\\n6. LARGE DATA: Use sklearn.utils.resample or Dask for out-of-core processing.\\n\\n7. SMALL DATA: Use LOOCV or repeated CV (10x 5-fold = 50 evaluations).\",\n  \"testing_plan\": \"TESTING PLAN: GRADUAL SCALING\\n\\nPHASE 1: MINI TESTING (3 examples, <5 min)\\n- Load mini_data_out.json\\n- Test feature computation: assert shape=(3,7), no NaN\\n- Test bootstrap with 100 samples: assert 0<=p<=1\\n- Test CV with 2-fold: assert finite R\u00b2\\n- Success: all assertions pass\\n\\nPHASE 2: MEDIUM TESTING (1,000 examples, ~30 min)\\n- Subsample 1,000 sentences\\n- Run bootstrap with 1,000 samples\\n- Check: completes in <5 min, no NaN, CI width reasonable\\n- Success: all checks pass\\n\\nPHASE 3: FULL PRODUCTION (13,129 examples, ~4-6 hrs)\\n- Run all 5 experiments with 10,000 bootstrap samples\\n- Exp 1: MSE test (2 datasets x 1 hr)\\n- Exp 2: Coefficient CI (2 datasets x 1 hr)\\n- Exp 3: CV (~10 min)\\n- Exp 4-5: Effect sizes + ablation (~30 min)\\n- Generate method_out.json\\n\\nVALIDATION:\\n1. p-values < 0.05 expected\\n2. R\u00b2 improvement positive for combined vs average\\n3. cv_syllables coefficient positive\\n4. No NaN or Inf in output\\n5. Correct sample sizes: WeeBIT=3,125, CEFR-SP=10,004\"\n}\n",

PAIRED BOOTSTRAP TEST for MSE reduction significance (10,000 samples)\\n2. BOOTSTRAP COEFFICIENT CI for Ridge regression coefficients\\n3. PROPER CROSS-VALIDATION with train/test separation\\n4. EFFECT SIZE ANALYSIS (R\u00b2 improvement, Cohen's d)\\n5. ABLATION STUDY (add-one-in, remove-one-out)\\n\\n```python\\nimport json, numpy as np, pandas as pd\\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import KFold\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error, r2_score\\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\\nimport pronouncing\\n\\n# Load datasets\\ndef load_datasets():\\n    with open('full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    sentences, scores, sources = [], [], []\\n    for dataset in data['datasets']:\\n        for ex in dataset['examples']:\\n            sentences.append(ex['input'])\\n            scores.append(float(ex['output']))\\n            sources.append(dataset['dataset'])\\n    return sentences, np.array(scores), np.array(sources)\\n\\nsentences, y, sources = load_datasets()\\n```\\n\\nFEATURES:\\n- avg_word_length, avg_syllables, avg_frequency (averages)\\n- cv_word_length, cv_syllables, cv_frequency (uniformity/coefficient of variation)\\n- sentence_length (word count)\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 1: Bootstrap MSE Test\\n```python\\ndef paired_bootstrap_mse_test(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n    np.random.seed(42)\\n    n = len(y)\\n    avg_feats = ['avg_word_length','avg_syllables','avg_frequency','sentence_length']\\n    unif_feats = ['cv_word_length','cv_syllables','cv_frequency']\\n    mse_diffs = []\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n, n, replace=True)\\n        oob = np.setdiff1d(np.arange(n), idx)\\n        if len(oob) < 10: continue\\n        sa = StandardScaler().fit(X.loc[idx, avg_feats])\\n        sb = StandardScaler().fit(X.loc[idx, avg_feats+unif_feats])\\n        mA = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(sa.transform(X.loc[idx,avg_feats]), y[idx])\\n        mB = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(sb.transform(X.loc[idx,avg_feats+unif_feats]), y[idx])\\n        mse_A = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mA.predict(sa.transform(X.loc[oob,avg_feats])))\\n        mse_B = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mB.predict(sb.transform(X.loc[oob,avg_feats+unif_feats])))\\n        mse_diffs.append(mse_A - mse_B)\\n    mse_diffs = np.array(mse_diffs)\\n    return {'p_value': np.mean(mse_diffs <= 0), 'ci_95': np.percentile(mse_diffs, [2.5, 97.5]).tolist(), 'mse_reduction_pct': np.mean(mse_diffs)/np.mean((y-np.mean(y))**2)*100}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 2: Bootstrap Coefficient CI\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coef_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n    np.random.seed(42)\\n    coefs = np.zeros((n_bootstrap, X.shape[1]))\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(len(y), len(y), replace=True)\\n        Xs = StandardScaler().fit_transform(X.iloc[idx])\\n        coefs[b] = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(Xs, y[idx]).coef_\\n    return pd.DataFrame([{'feature': f, 'mean_coef': np.mean(coefs[:,i]), 'ci_95': np.percentile(coefs[:,i], [2.5, 97.5]).tolist(), 'significant': (np.percentile(coefs[:,i],2.5)>0) if np.mean(coefs[:,i])>0 else (np.percentile(coefs[:,i],97.5)<0)} for i,f in enumerate(X.columns)])\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 3: Cross-Validation\\n```python\\ndef cv_evaluate(X, y):\\n    kf = KFold(5, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\\n    r2_folds, mse_folds = [], []\\n    for train_idx, test_idx in kf.split(X):\\n        scaler = StandardScaler().fit(X.iloc[train_idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(scaler.transform(X.iloc[train_idx]), y[train_idx])\\n        y_pred = model.predict(scaler.transform(X.iloc[test_idx]))\\n        r2_folds.append(r2_score(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n        mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n    return {'test_r2_mean': np.mean(r2_folds), 'test_r2_sd': np.std(r2_folds), 'test_mse_mean': np.mean(mse_folds), 'test_mse_sd': np.std(mse_folds)}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 4-5: Effect sizes and ablation\\n- np.mean(mse_diffs)/np.mean((y-np.mean(y))**2)*100}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 2: Bootstrap Coefficient CI\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coef_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n    np.random.seed(42)\\n    coefs     coefs[b] = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(Xs, y[idx]).coef_\\n    return pd.DataFrame([{'feature': f, 'mean_coef': np.mean(coefs[:,i]), 'ci_95': np.percentile(coefs[:,i], [2.5, 97.5]).tolist(), Cross-Validation\\n```python\\ndef cv_evaluate(X, y):\\n    kf = KFold(5, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\\n    r2_folds, mse_folds = [], []\\n    for train_idx, test_idx in kf.split(X):\\n        scaler = StandardScaler().fit(X.iloc[train_idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(scaler.transform(X.iloc[train_idx]), y[train_idx])\\n        y_pred = model.predict(scaler.transform(X.iloc[test_idx]))\\n        r2_folds.append(r2_score(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n        mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n    return {'test_r2_mean': np.mean(r2_folds), 'test_r2_sd': np.std(r2_folds), 'test_mse_mean': np.mean(mse_folds), 'test_mse_sd': np.std(mse_folds)}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 4-5: Effect sizes and ablation\\n- Compute R\u00b2 difference with bootstrap CI\\n- Cohen's d = 2*r/sqrt(1-r\u00b2) where r=sqrt(R\u00b2)\\n- Ablation: test each uniformity feature individually\\n\\nOUTPUT: method_out.json with all results.\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"FALLBACK STRATEGIES\\n\\n1. Check that all tables have reasonable values (no NaN, no Inf)\\n5. Verify sample sizes: WeeBIT (3,125), CEFR-SP (10,004), total (13,129)\\n\\n### Red Flags to Watch For\\n\\n1. **Bootstrap p-value = 0 or 1**: Indicates insufficient bootstrap samples or bug in code\\n2. **Coefficient CI includes both very large positive and negative values**: Indicates numerical instability or insufficient data\\n3. **R\u00b2 is negative**: Indicates model is worse than baseline (mean prediction);
