  "file_text": "{\n  \"title\": \"Statistical evaluation of uniformity features for readability\",\n  \"summary\": \"Comprehensive statistical evaluation of the Uniformity Principle hypothesis: bootstrap significance tests for MSE reduction, feature coefficient uncertainty quantification, proper train/test reporting, effect size analysis, and ablation studies.\",\n  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"cpu_light\",\n  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"EXPERIMENT OVERVIEW\\n\\nThis experiment evaluates the Uniformity Principle hypothesis using WeeBIT (3,125 sentences) and CEFR-SP (10,004 sentences) datasets. Five statistical tests are conducted:\\n\\n1. PAIRED BOOTSTRAP TEST: Test MSE reduction (17.8% WeeBIT, 8.9% CEFR-SP) with 10,000 bootstrap samples\\n2. COEFFICIENT CI: Bootstrap 95% confidence intervals for Ridge regression coefficients  \\n3. PROPER CV: 5-fold cross-validation with train/test separation (report test metrics only)\\n4. EFFECT SIZE: R\u00b2 improvement with 95% CI, Cohen's d for practical significance\\n5. ABLATION: Add-one-in and remove-one-out uniformity feature analysis\\n\\nKEY IMPLEMENTATION DETAILS:\\n\\n```python\\nimport json, numpy as np, pandas as pd\\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import KFold\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error, r2_score\\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\\nimport pronouncing  # CMUdict for syllable counting\\n\\n# Load datasets from dependency artifact (full_data_out.json)\\ndef load_datasets():\\n    with open('full_data_out.json', 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    sentences, scores, sources = [], [], []\\n    for dataset in data['datasets']:\\n        for ex in dataset['examples']:\\n            sentences.append(ex['input'])\\n            scores.append(float(ex['output']))\\n            sources.append(dataset['dataset'])\\n    return sentences, np.array(scores), np.array(sources)\\n\\nsentences, y, sources = load_datasets()\\nprint(f'Loaded {len(sentences)} sentences')\\n```\\n\\nFEATURES TO COMPUTE:\\n- avg_word_length, avg_syllables, avg_frequency (average features)\\n- cv_word_length, cv_syllables, cv_frequency (uniformity features)\\n- sentence_length\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 1: PAIRED BOOTSTRAP MSE TEST\\n```python\\ndef paired_bootstrap_mse_test(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n    np.random.seed(42)\\n    n = len(y)\\n    avg_feats = ['avg_word_length','avg_syllables','avg_frequency','sentence_length']\\n    unif_feats = ['cv_word_length','cv_syllables','cv_frequency']\\n    combined = avg_feats + unif_feats\\n    mse_diffs = []\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n, n, replace=True)\\n        oob = np.setdiff1d(np.arange(n), idx)\\n        if len(oob) < 10: continue\\n        sa = StandardScaler().fit(X.loc[idx, avg_feats])\\n        sb = StandardScaler().fit(X.loc[idx, combined])\\n        mA = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(sa.transform(X.loc[idx,avg_feats]), y[idx])\\n        mB = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(sb.transform(X.loc[idx,combined]), y[idx])\\n        mse_A = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mA.predict(sa.transform(X.loc[oob,avg_feats])))\\n        mse_B = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mB.predict(sb.transform(X.loc[oob,combined])))\\n        mse_diffs.append(mse_A - mse_B)\\n    mse_diffs = np.array(mse_diffs)\\n    return {\\n        'p_value_one_sided': np.mean(mse_diffs <= 0),\\n        'ci_95': (np.percentile(mse_diffs,2.5), np.percentile(mse_diffs,97.5)),\\n        'mse_reduction_pct': (np.mean(mse_diffs)/np.mean((y-np.mean(y))**2))*100\\n    }\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 2: BOOTSTRAP COEFFICIENT CI\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coef_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n    np.random.seed(42)\\n    n, p = len(y), X.shape[1]\\n    coefs = np.zeros((n_bootstrap, p))\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n, n, replace=True)\\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\\n        Xs = scaler.fit_transform(X.iloc[idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(Xs, y[idx])\\n        coefs[b] = model.coef_\\n    results = []\\n    for i, f in enumerate(X.columns):\\n        c = coefs[:,i]\\n        results.append({'feature': f, 'mean_coef': np.mean(c),\\n            'ci_95': (np.percentile(c,2.5), np.percentile(c,97.5)),\\n            'significant': (np.percentile(c,2.5)>0) if np.mean(c)>0 else (np.percentile(c,97.5)<0)})\\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 3: CROSS-VALIDATION (TRAIN/TEST SEPARATION)\\n```python\\ndef cv_evaluate(X, y, n_splits=5):\\n    kf = KFold(n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\\n    r2_folds, mse_folds = [], []\\n    for train_idx, test_idx in kf.split(X):\\n        scaler = StandardScaler().fit(X.iloc[train_idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(scaler.transform(X.iloc[train_idx]), y[train_idx])\\n        y_pred = model.predict(scaler.transform(X.iloc[test_idx]))\\n        r2_folds.append(r2_score(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n        mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n    return {'test_r2_mean': np.mean(r2_folds), 'test_r2_sd': np.std(r2_folds),\\n            'test_mse_mean': np.mean(mse_folds), 'test_mse_sd': np.std(mse_folds)}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 4: EFFECT SIZE ANALYSIS\\n- Compute R\u00b2 difference (combined - average) with bootstrap 95% CI\\n- Convert R\u00b2 to correlation: r = sqrt(R\u00b2)\\n- Compute Cohen's d: d = 2r / sqrt(1 - r^2)\\n- Interpretation: d=0.2 (small), 0.5 (medium), 0.8 (large)\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 5: ABLATION STUDY\\n- Baseline: average features only\\n- Add-one-in: average + one uniformity feature at a time\\n- Remove-one-out: combined minus one uniformity feature at a time\\n- Report R\u00b2 for each condition\\n\\nOUTPUT: method_out.json with all results in publication-ready format.\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"FALLBACK STRATEGIES FOR COMMON ISSUES\\n\\n1. SLOW BOOTSTRAP: If 10,000 bootstrap samples take too long, reduce to 1,000 samples (still valid per statistical literature). Alternative: use permutation test with 999 permutations (faster than bootstrap).\\n\\n2. CMUDICT OOV: If pronouncing library has high out-of-vocabulary rate for syllable counting, use heuristic fallback: count vowel groups (a,e,i,o,u,y) with silent-e adjustment (subtract 1 if word ends in 'e').\\n\\n3. NO SUBTLEX-US: If SUBTLEX-US word frequency norms are unavailable, use NLTK Gutenberg frequencies: from nltk.corpus import gutenberg; freq = Counter(gutenberg.words()); normalize as log(1+count)/total_words.\\n\\n4. MULTICOLLINEARITY: If Ridge coefficients have high variance (wide bootstrap CI), check VIF. If VIF>10, remove correlated features. Alternative: use Lasso for feature selection then refit with OLS on selected features.\\n\\n5. WIDE BOOTSTRAP CI: If bootstrap CI includes 0 despite expected significance, use BCa (bias-corrected accelerated) bootstrap via scipy.stats.bootstrap(method='BCa').\\n\\n6. LARGE DATASETS: If scaling beyond 13,129 sentences, use incremental processing with sklearn.utils.resample or Dask for out-of-core computation.\\n\\n7. unif_feats\\n    mse_diffs = []\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n, n, replace=True)\\n        oob = np.setdiff1d(np.arange(n), idx)\\n        if len(oob) < 10: continue\\n        sa = StandardScaler().fit(X.loc[idx, avg_feats])\\n        sb = StandardScaler().fit(X.loc[idx, combined])\\n        mA = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(sa.transform(X.loc[idx,avg_feats]), y[idx])\\n        mB = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(sb.transform(X.loc[idx,combined]), y[idx])\\n        mse_A = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mA.predict(sa.transform(X.loc[oob,avg_feats])))\\n        mse_B = mean_squared_error(y[oob], mB.predict(sb.transform(X.loc[oob,combined])))\\n        mse_diffs.append(mse_A - mse_B)\\n    mse_diffs = np.array(mse_diffs)\\n    return {\\n        'p_value_one_sided': np.mean(mse_diffs <= 0),\\n        'ci_95': (np.percentile(mse_diffs,2.5), np.percentile(mse_diffs,97.5)),\\n        'mse_reduction_pct': (np.mean(mse_diffs)/np.mean((y-np.mean(y))**2))*100\\n    }\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 2: BOOTSTRAP COEFFICIENT CI\\n```python\\ndef bootstrap_coef_ci(X, y, n_bootstrap=10000):\\n    np.random.seed(42)\\n    n, p = len(y), X.shape[1]\\n    coefs = np.zeros((n_bootstrap, p))\\n    for b in range(n_bootstrap):\\n        idx = np.random.choice(n, n, replace=True)\\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\\n        Xs = scaler.fit_transform(X.iloc[idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(Xs, y[idx])\\n        coefs[b] = model.coef_\\n    results = []\\n    for i, f in enumerate(X.columns):\\n        c = coefs[:,i]\\n        results.append({'feature': f, 'mean_coef': np.mean(c),\\n            'ci_95': (np.percentile(c,2.5), np.percentile(c,97.5)),\\n            'significant': (np.percentile(c,2.5)>0) if np.mean(c)>0 else (np.percentile(c,97.5)<0)})\\n    return pd.DataFrame(results)\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 3: CROSS-VALIDATION (TRAIN/TEST SEPARATION)\\n```python\\ndef cv_evaluate(X, y, n_splits=5):\\n    kf = KFold(n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\\n    r2_folds, mse_folds = [], []\\n    for train_idx, test_idx in kf.split(X):\\n        scaler = StandardScaler().fit(X.iloc[train_idx])\\n        model = Ridge(1.0, random_state=42).fit(scaler.transform(X.iloc[train_idx]), y[train_idx])\\n        y_pred = model.predict(scaler.transform(X.iloc[test_idx]))\\n        r2_folds.append(r2_score(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n        mse_folds.append(mean_squared_error(y[test_idx], y_pred))\\n    return {'test_r2_mean': np.mean(r2_folds), 'test_r2_sd': np.std(r2_folds),\\n            'test_mse_mean': np.mean(mse_folds), 'test_mse_sd': np.std(mse_folds)}\\n```\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 4: EFFECT SIZE ANALYSIS\\n- Compute R\u00b2 difference (combined - average) with bootstrap 95% CI\\n- Convert R\u00b2 to correlation: r = sqrt(R\u00b2)\\n- Compute Cohen's d: d = 2r / sqrt(1 - r^2)\\n- Interpretation: d=0.2 (small), 0.5 (medium), 0.8 (large)\\n\\nEXPERIMENT 5: ABLATION STUDY\\n- Baseline: average features only\\n- Add-one-in: average + one uniformity feature at a time\\n- Remove-one-out: combined minus one uniformity feature at a time\\n- Report R\u00b2 for each condition\\n\\nOUTPUT: method_out.json with all results in publication-ready format.\",\n     6\t  \"fallback_plan\": \"FALLBACK STRATEGIES FOR COMMON ISSUES\\n\\n1. SLOW BOOTSTRAP: If 10,000 bootstrap samples take too long, reduce to 1,000 samples (still valid per statistical literature). Alternative: use permutation test with 999 permutations (faster than bootstrap).\\n\\n2. CMUDICT OOV: If pronouncing library has high out-of-vocabulary rate for syllable counting, use heuristic fallback: count vowel groups (a,e,i,o,u,y) with silent-e adjustment (subtract 1 if word ends in 'e').\\n\\n3. NO SUBTLEX-US: If SUBTLEX-US word frequency norms are unavailable, use NLTK Gutenberg frequencies: from nltk.corpus import gutenberg; freq = Counter(gutenberg.words()); normalize as log(1+count)/total_words.\\n\\n4. MULTICOLLINEARITY: If Ridge coefficients have high variance (wide bootstrap CI), check VIF. If VIF>10, remove correlated features. Alternative: use Lasso for feature selection then refit with OLS on selected features.\\n\\n5. WIDE BOOTSTRAP CI: If bootstrap CI includes 0 despite expected significance, use BCa (bias-corrected accelerated) bootstrap via scipy.stats.bootstrap(method='BCa').\\n\\n6. LARGE DATASETS: If scaling beyond 13,129 sentences, use incremental processing with sklearn.utils.resample or Dask for out-of-core computation.\\n\\n7. INSUFFICIENT DATA: If using subset with <100 samples, use LOOCV (leave-one-out) or repeated CV (10\u00d7 5-fold = 50 evaluations) for more stable estimates.\",\n     7\t  \"testing_plan\": \"TESTING PLAN: GRADUAL SCALING PATTERN\\n\\nPHASE 1: MINI DATASET TESTING (3 examples, <5 minutes)\\n- Load mini_data_out.json (3 sentences)\\n- Test feature computation: assert shape=(3,7), no NaN values\\n- Test bootstrap MSE test with n_bootstrap=100: assert 0<=p_value<=1\\n- Test coefficient CI with n_bootstrap=100: assert all features have valid CI\\n- Test CV with 2-fold: assert finite R\u00b2 and MSE values\\n- Test ablation: assert results DataFrame has >=3 rows\\n- Success criteria: all tests pass without errors\\n\\nPHASE 2: MEDIUM DATASET TESTING (1,000 examples, ~30 minutes)\\n- Subsample 1,000 from full dataset (use stratified sampling by score)\\n- Run bootstrap with n_bootstrap=1,000 (reduced from 10,000)\\n- Check: completes in <5 minutes (implies <1 hour for full 10,000)\\n- Check: no NaN or Inf in p-value\\n- Check: CI width in reasonable range (0 < width < 1)\\n- Check: coefficient signs interpretable (cv_syllables should be positive)\\n- Success criteria: all checks pass\\n\\nPHASE 3: FULL PRODUCTION RUN (13,129 examples, ~4-6 hours)\\n- Run Experiments 1-5 with n_bootstrap=10,000\\n- Experiment 1: Bootstrap MSE test (2 datasets \u00d7 ~1 hour)\\n- Experiment 2: Coefficient CI (2 datasets \u00d7 ~1 hour)\\n- Experiment 3: CV evaluation (~10 minutes)\\n- Experiment 4: Effect sizes (~1 minute)\\n- Experiment 5: Ablation (~30 minutes)\\n- Generate method_out.json with all results\\n\\nVALIDATION CHECKS AFTER PRODUCTION:\\n1. p-values should be <0.05 (hypothesis predicts MSE reduction with uniformity features)\\n2. R\u00b2 improvement positive for combined vs average-only model\\n3. cv_syllables coefficient positive (lower CV = easier reading = higher score if 0=easy, 1=hard)\\n4.
